### [186] [Models Can Model, But Can't Bind: Structured Grounding in Text-to-Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21751)
*Zhiqi Gao,Albert Ge,Alexander Berenbeim,Nathaniel D. Bastian,Frederic Sala*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究提出Text2Opt-Bench基准，评估文本到优化的建模与绑定能力。发现随着实例数据规模增大，模型准确率显著下降，提出有效绑定极限（effective binding limit）。为此设计BIND方法，在推理时将数值数据外部化至结构文件，使模型通过程序化方式绑定数据而非从提示中转录。BIND显著提升GPT-5-Nano和GPT-5的准确率，并在低token成本下达到更高性能。进一步验证表明，仅针对绑定任务微调的专用模型优于端到端训练模型，1.5B绑定专家模型可媲美7B端到端基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有文本到优化模型在处理大规模实例数据时准确率严重下降，核心问题在于‘绑定’能力受限，即难以正确将系数、参数等与具体问题数据关联。需要更有效的绑定机制以提升模型泛化能力。

Method: 构建Text2Opt-Bench基准，涵盖12类优化问题；提出推理时外部化数据的BIND方法，将数值数据存储于结构文件中，由模型程序化绑定；对比不同微调策略，包括仅针对绑定任务的专用模型与端到端微调模型。

Result: BIND使GPT-5-Nano准确率从59.1%提升至82.4%，接近pass@5性能但消耗更低token；GPT-5准确率从86.2%提升至95.8%。1.5B绑定专用模型在三类结构不同的优化任务上超越7B端到端模型。

Conclusion: 绑定是文本到优化中的关键瓶颈，通过外部化数据并采用程序化绑定可显著提升模型性能。专用绑定模型在效率与效果上均优于端到端训练，证明了分离建模与绑定任务的有效性。

Abstract: Text-to-optimization requires two separable capabilities: modeling -- choosing the right optimization structure -- and binding -- grounding every coefficient, index, and parameter in the concrete problem data. We study this via Text2Opt-Bench, a scalable benchmark of solver-verified optimization problems spanning 12 categories, from textbook linear programs to stochastic and multi-objective formulations with up to thousands of variables. Across 10+ models, we find that accuracy collapses as instance data grows, even when the formulation itself is simple. We call this the effective binding limit. We address this via a simple inference-time approach, BIND, which externalizes numeric data to structured files so the model binds data programmatically rather than transcribing from the prompt. BIND improves GPT-5-Nano from 59.1% to 82.4% accuracy, matching pass@5 (82.0%) at lower token cost than pass@1, and GPT-5 from 86.2% to 95.8%. Furthermore, we validate our hypothesis by finetuning a model exclusively on binding and show that it outperforms end-to-end SFT and RL across three structurally distinct optimization categories, with a 1.5B binding specialist alone matching a 7B end-to-end baseline.

### [187] [PEARL: Unbiased Percentile Estimation via Contrastive Learning for Industrial-Scale Livestream Recommendation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21752)
*Blake Gella,Wei Wu,Yuhao Yin,Zexi Huang,Zikai Wang,Emily Liu,Junlin Zhang,Wentao Guo,Qinglei Wang*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 用户交互数据中的行为强度不平衡导致反馈信号失真，使模型过度放大高活跃用户信号而忽略低活跃用户，降低推荐质量与鲁棒性。

Method: 提出PEARL框架，基于相对优势去偏，利用真实对比交互样本直接近似百分位关系，无需辅助分布估计；引入基于预测的自举机制进行百分位平滑，结合广义加权形式与协同训练策略增强灵活性与表征学习能力。

Result: 离线实验显示PEARL有效缓解行为偏差并提升多目标排名性能；线上A/B测试在亿级用户直播平台验证显著收益：观看时长+2.10%，消费金额+0.80%，互动率+1.49%，举报率-6.91%。

Conclusion: PEARL通过建模相对偏好而非绝对行为强度，成功应对行为强度不平衡问题，在真实场景中显著提升推荐系统性能与用户体验。

Abstract: Recommender systems trained on user interaction data are susceptible to behavioral intensity imbalance--a systematic distortion arising from heterogeneous engagement patterns across users. This imbalance skews feedback signals such that observed interactions no longer faithfully reflect true preferences, causing models to disproportionately amplify signals from highly active users while underrepresenting others, which ultimately degrades recommendation quality and robustness at scale. To address this issue, we propose a nonparametric contrastive percentile approximation framework, PEARL, that models relative preference signals instead of absolute engagement magnitudes. Building upon relative advantage debiasing, PEARL leverages real contrastive interaction samples to approximate percentile relationships directly, without relying on auxiliary distribution estimation models. We provide theoretical justification demonstrating that such pairwise comparisons yield unbiased estimates of percentile-based preference signals. For broader applicability, we introduce a prediction-based bootstrapping mechanism for percentile smoothing to handle sparse and discrete feedback, alongside a generalized value-weighted formulation and a co-training strategy to enhance both modeling flexibility and representation learning. Extensive offline experiments demonstrate that PEARL effectively mitigates behavioral bias and consistently improves recommendation performance across multiple ranking targets. Deployed in a production livestream platform with a combined user base of billions, online A/B testing confirms substantial real-world gains: +2.10% Watch Duration, +0.80% Consumption Amount, +1.49% Interaction Rate, and -6.91% Report Rate.

### [188] [Machine learning prediction of obstructive coronary artery disease using opportunistic coronary calcium and epicardial fat assessments from CT calcium scoring scans](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21762)
*Juhwan Lee,Ammar Hoori,Tao Hu,Justin N. Kim,Mohamed H. E. Makhlouf,Michelle C. Williams,David E. Newby,Robert Gilkeson,Sanjay Rajagopalan,David L. Wilson*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究开发了一种基于机器学习的先进框架，利用非增强CT钙化评分（CTCS）图像中的冠状动脉钙化和心外膜脂肪定量分析，预测阻塞性冠状动脉疾病（CAD）。通过结合CatBoost与SHAP值进行特征选择，从424个候选特征中筛选出14个最具预测性的特征，其中前两位来自脂肪组学特征，其余12个来自钙化组学特征。优化模型表现出优异的预测性能：敏感性83.1±4.6%，特异性93.8±1.7%，准确率85.3±2.0%，F1分数73.9±3.3%。该方法显著提升了预测效果，尤其在钙化评分为零但存在阻塞性CAD的患者中仍具可靠性，有望改善临床决策，减少对增强扫描或侵入性检查的依赖，适用于低至中等风险人群。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有非增强CT钙化评分虽能有效检测冠状动脉钙化，但在预测阻塞性冠状动脉疾病方面存在局限，尤其在钙化评分较低或为零的情况下容易漏诊。因此亟需一种更精准的预测方法，整合更多影像组学特征以提升诊断效能。

Method: 研究采用多模态数据融合策略，从SCOT-HEART试验中1,324名患者的CTCS与冠状动脉CT血管造影数据中提取24项临床变量、189项钙化组学特征及211项心外膜脂肪组学特征。通过CatBoost算法结合SHAP值进行特征选择，识别关键预测因子，并使用CatBoost梯度提升方法构建预测模型，最终评估其在不同钙化水平患者中的表现。

Result: 从424个特征中筛选出14个最优特征，其中脂肪组学特征贡献前两名；模型在预测阻塞性CAD上达到高敏感性（83.1±4.6%）、高特异性（93.8±1.7%）、高准确率（85.3±2.0%）及良好F1分数（73.9±3.3%），且在零钙化评分患者中仍具备可靠预测能力。加入钙化和脂肪组学特征显著提升模型性能。

Conclusion: 基于CTCS影像的钙化与心外膜脂肪组学特征融合的机器学习模型可显著提高阻塞性冠状动脉疾病的预测能力，尤其适用于低至中等风险人群，具有潜力减少对额外对比剂或侵入性检查的需求，推动精准心血管影像学发展。

Abstract: Non-contrast computed tomography calcium scoring (CTCS) is a cost-effective imaging modality widely used to detect coronary artery calcifications. This study aimed to develop an advanced machine learning framework that utilizes quantitative analyses of coronary calcium and epicardial fat from CTCS images to predict obstructive coronary artery disease (CAD). The study population consisted of 1,324 patients from the SCOT-HEART clinical trial who underwent both CTCS and coronary CT angiography. We extracted and analyzed a broad range of features, including 24 clinical variables, 189 calcium-omics, and 211 epicardial fat-omics features from the CTCS images. Feature selection was conducted using the CatBoost algorithm combined with SHapley Additive exPlanation (SHAP) values. Predictive modeling utilized the CatBoost gradient boosting method, focusing on the most informative features. From an initial set of 424 candidate features, 14 were identified as most predictive through the CatBoost-SHAP method. The top two predictive features originated from fat-omics, with the remaining 12 features derived from calcium-omics. The optimized model achieved robust predictive capabilities, demonstrating a sensitivity of 83.1+/-4.6%, specificity of 93.8+/-1.7%, accuracy of 85.3+/-2.0%, and an F1 score of 73.9+/-3.3%. Inclusion of calcium-omics and fat-omics data significantly improved predictive performance. Notably, the model also showed reliable predictive accuracy in patients with diverse coronary calcium scores, including cases with obstructive CAD despite a zero-calcium score. This innovative approach holds promise for improving clinical decision-making and potentially reducing dependence on contrast-enhanced or invasive diagnostic procedures, particularly within low-to intermediate-risk patient groups.

### [189] [On the Sample Complexity of Discounted Reinforcement Learning with Optimized Certainty Equivalents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21763)
*Oliver Mortensen,Mohammad Sadegh Talebi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究有限折扣马尔可夫决策过程中的风险敏感强化学习，假设存在生成模型。考虑一类称为优化确定等价（OCE）的风险度量，包括熵风险、条件风险价值（CVaR）和均值-方差等。重点分析在递归OCE下学习最优状态-动作值函数（值学习）和最优策略（策略学习）的样本复杂性。文章给出了使对应OCE目标可实现概率近似正确（PAC）学习的效用函数$u$的精确刻画，并分析了一种简单的基于模型的方法，推导出PAC样本复杂性界。证明当$u$的定义域不为全实数集（即$\text{dom}(u)\neq \mathbb{R}$）时，问题不可PAC学习。同时建立了值学习与策略学习的下界，表明在状态-动作空间大小$SA$上的紧性；对更受限的一类效用函数，进一步得到了依赖有效时长远的下界，尤其对于$\text{CVaR}_τ$，揭示了其对$τ$的正确依赖关系为$\frac{1}{τ^2}$，相较于现有最优结果改进了$\\frac{1}{τ}$因子，尽管在$\\frac{1}{1-γ}$上的依赖仍非最优。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究风险敏感强化学习在有限折扣MDP中的样本复杂性，尤其是在存在生成模型的前提下，理解不同风险度量（如CVaR、熵风险等）下的学习可行性与效率，推动风险感知智能体在不确定环境中的可靠学习。

Method: 采用基于模型的方法，分析递归优化确定等价（OCE）风险度量下的值学习与策略学习问题，通过构建理论框架，推导样本复杂性上界与下界，结合效用函数的定义域性质进行可学习性分析。

Result: 当且仅当效用函数$u$具有全实数域（$\text{dom}(u) = \\mathbb{R}$）时，对应的OCE目标才是PAC可学习的；对$\text{CVaR}_τ$，样本复杂性对$τ$的依赖为$\\frac{1}{τ^2}$，优于已有结果；下界显示在$SA$和$\\frac{1}{1-γ}$上的依赖是紧的，且在特定类别的效用函数中可显式刻画有效时长远的影响。

Conclusion: 本工作首次对递归OCE风险度量下的风险敏感强化学习提供了完整的样本复杂性理论分析，揭示了可学习性的关键条件——效用函数必须定义在整个实数域上，并明确了$\text{CVaR}_τ$等重要风险度量的最优样本复杂性依赖结构，为设计高效、鲁棒的风险敏感学习算法提供了理论基础。

Abstract: We study risk-sensitive reinforcement learning in finite discounted MDPs, where a generative model of the MDP is assumed to be available. We consider a family or risk measures called the optimized certainty equivalent (OCE), which includes important risk measures such as entropic risk, CVaR, and mean-variance. Our focus is on the sample complexities of learning the optimal state-action value function (value learning) and an optimal policy (policy learning) under recursive OCE. We provide an exact characterization of utility functions $u$ for which the corresponding OCE defines an objective that is PAC-learnable. We analyze a simple model-based approach and derive PAC sample complexity bounds. We establish that whenever $u$ does not have full domain $\text{dom}(u)\neq \mathbb{R}$, the corresponding problem is not PAC-learnable. Finally, we establish corresponding lower bounds for both value and policy learning, demonstrating tightness in the size $SA$ of state-action space, and for a more restricted class of utilities, we derive lower bounds that makes the dependence on the effective horizon $\frac{1}{1-γ}$ explicit. Specifically, for $\text{CVaR}_τ$ we show that the correct dependence on $τ$ is $\frac{1}{τ^2}$, thus improving by a factor of $\frac{1}τ$ over state-of-the-art although our bound has a suboptimal dependence on $\frac{1}{1-γ}$.

### [190] [Provable Robustness against Backdoor Attacks via the Primal-Dual Perspective on Differential Privacy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21780)
*Aman Saxena,Jan Schuchardt,Yan Scholten,Stephan Günnemann*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种将随机平滑与差分隐私的对偶视角相结合的新框架，通过隐私轮廓实现异构机制的组合，从而在训练和推理阶段联合分析对抗性攻击（包括后门攻击），实现了对复杂威胁模型下鲁棒性的端到端认证。该框架利用现有差分隐私机制的分析结果，为DP-SGD与推理时平滑相结合的复合机制提供了紧致的联合鲁棒性保证，并在MNIST和CIFAR-10上验证了其有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有随机平滑方法难以同时应对训练时和推理时的联合攻击（如后门攻击），缺乏统一的鲁棒性证书来涵盖训练和测试阶段的共同扰动，因此需要一种能够整合不同机制、支持复杂威胁建模的通用认证框架。

Method: 将随机平滑与差分隐私的对偶视图结合，引入隐私轮廓作为数值化工具，用于组合不同类型的随机机制；利用已有的差分隐私分析技术，构建模块化、可组合的鲁棒性认证框架，实现对训练-测试联合扰动的联合保障。

Result: 成功推导出基于DP-SGD与推理时平滑的联合鲁棒性保证，在MNIST和CIFAR-10数据集上验证了该框架的有效性，显著提升了对复杂攻击场景的防御能力。

Conclusion: 本文提出了一种通用且原则性的框架，可用于通过复合机制认证面对现实世界复杂攻击模型的鲁棒性，为安全机器学习中的多阶段攻击防护提供了新思路。

Abstract: Randomized smoothing is a powerful tool for certifying robustness to adversarial perturbations, including poisoning attacks via randomized training and evasion attacks via randomized inference. Extending these guarantees to backdoor attacks, where training and test data are jointly perturbed, remains challenging because training- and test-time randomized mechanisms must be analyzed within a single robustness certificate. We address this by connecting randomized smoothing to the dual view of differential privacy through privacy profiles, which provide a numerical procedure for composing heterogeneous mechanisms. The resulting framework enables tight, modular, end-to-end certification of complex, composed mechanisms while leveraging existing analyses of differentially private mechanisms. We instantiate the framework for DP-SGD and Deep Partition Aggregation with inference-time smoothing, deriving joint robustness guarantees against both training-time and inference-time attacks. Experiments on MNIST and CIFAR-10 demonstrate the effectiveness of our framework. Overall, we provide a principled and general framework for using composite mechanisms to certify robustness under complex threat models that better capture the capabilities of real-world adversaries.

### [191] [MMD-Balls as Credal Sets: A PAC-Bayesian Framework for Epistemic Uncertainty in Test-Time Adaptation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21783)
*Ahanaf Hasan Ariq*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于PAC-Bayesian框架的测试时自适应（TTA）方法，通过最大均值差异（MMD）显式建模分布偏移对预测可靠性的影响。核心贡献是将MMD球解释为Walley模糊概率理论中的可信集，从而实现自然的主观不确定性量化。研究建立了：(i) 在RKHS-Lipschitz损失假设下依赖MMD的泛化边界；(ii) 基于MMD集中性的有限样本版本；(iii) 可信集中所有分布的最坏情况风险统一界，包含上下界分解；(iv) 保测地线性约束，解释核引导自适应如何保护局部特征几何结构。该框架区分了主观与固有不确定性，并提供了一个合理的自适应决策准则。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有测试时自适应（TTA）方法虽能提升模型在分布偏移下的性能，但缺乏形式化保证来连接分布偏移程度与预测可靠性之间的关系。亟需一种能够量化不确定性并指导是否进行自适应的理论框架。

Method: 提出一个PAC-Bayesian框架，将最大均值差异（MMD）作为分布偏移的度量，并将其对应的MMD球解释为可信集（credal set），基于沃尔利（Walley）模糊概率理论构建不确定性量化机制。引入RKHS-Lipschitz损失假设，推导出依赖于MMD的泛化边界；利用MMD集中不等式获得有限样本结果；建立可信集上的最坏情况风险上界，并分析其上下界分解；进一步提出保测地线性约束以解释核引导自适应对局部几何结构的保护作用。

Result: 成功建立了基于MMD的可解释、可计算的泛化边界；实现了对主观不确定性的自然量化；提出了可信集框架下的最优决策准则；揭示了核引导自适应在保持局部特征结构方面的几何优势。实验表明该方法能有效判断何时应进行自适应，并提高模型鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 本工作通过将MMD球解释为可信集，首次在理论上将测试时自适应中的分布偏移与不确定性量化相结合，为自适应决策提供了严谨依据。该框架不仅提升了模型可靠性，还为未来鲁棒学习中的不确定性管理提供了新范式。

Abstract: Test-time adaptation (TTA) methods improve model performance under distribution shift but lack formal guarantees connecting shift magnitude to prediction reliability. We develop a PAC-Bayesian framework yielding generalization bounds explicitly parameterized by the maximum mean discrepancy (MMD) between source and target distributions. Our principal contribution is interpreting MMD-balls around the source distribution as credal sets in Walley's imprecise probability theory, yielding natural epistemic uncertainty quantification. We establish: (i) a PAC-Bayesian bound with an MMD-dependent shift penalty under an RKHS-Lipschitz loss assumption; (ii) a finite-sample version via MMD concentration; (iii) a uniform worst-case risk bound over all distributions in the credal set, with a lower-upper risk decomposition; and (iv) geodesic preservation bounds explaining why kernel-guided adaptation protects local feature geometry. The credal set interpretation separates epistemic from aleatoric uncertainty and provides a principled decision criterion for when adaptation is warranted.

</details>


### [192] [Three Costs of Amortizing Gaussian Process Inference with Neural Processes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21798)
*Robin Young*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文研究了神经过程（Neural Processes）如何近似高斯过程（Gaussian Process）的推断，通过一个学习得到的O(n)映射替代了精确的O(n³)后验。作者为一类潜在神经过程（LNP）提供了从高斯过程到LNP预测之间的KL散度上界，并将其分解为三个可解释的来源：标签污染（因神经过程使用标签值估计原本与标签无关的量）、信息瓶颈（有限维度表示无法完全捕捉上下文几何结构）以及共享编码器带来的摊销误差。其中，瓶颈截断项随表示维度d呈指数或幂律衰减，与核函数平滑性和输入维度相关；标签污染项在一般情况下为O(1)，仅观测噪声部分以O(1/n)衰减，表明通过标签依赖表示进行不确定性估计存在持续代价。研究结果揭示了该类方法中摊销机制的成本，并提出改进建议：仅用上下文位置预测方差、用二阶池化替代均值聚合以缩小主要摊销差距。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在理解神经过程在近似高斯过程时的误差来源，特别是其摊销推理机制所带来的系统性偏差，从而指导模型架构设计以更准确地捕捉不确定性。

Method: 通过理论分析，对一类潜在神经过程（LNP）建立高斯过程与LNP预测之间KL散度的上界，并将该上界分解为三个组成部分：标签污染、信息瓶颈和摊销误差。利用核函数特性（如平方指数核和Matérn-ν核）推导不同成分的渐近行为，结合表示维度与输入维度的关系分析其收敛速度。

Result: 发现信息瓶颈项随表示维度增长快速衰减（指数或幂律），而标签污染项在多数情况下保持常数，仅观测噪声部分随样本数增加而减小。这表明标签依赖的表示方式引入了不可忽略的系统性偏差。此外，提出通过仅基于上下文位置预测方差、采用二阶池化代替均值聚合等架构改进策略，可有效减少主导的摊销误差。

Conclusion: 该研究系统刻画了神经过程在高斯过程近似中的关键误差来源，明确了架构设计对性能的影响机制，提出了具有理论依据的改进方案，有助于提升不确定性建模的准确性。

Abstract: Neural processes amortize Gaussian process inference, replacing the exact $O(n^3)$ posterior with a learned $O(n)$ map from context sets to predictive distributions. For a class of latent neural processes, we bound the Kullback--Leibler (KL) divergence between the GP and LNP predictives, decomposing it into three interpretable sources, namely label contamination as the neural process uses label values to estimate a quantity that is label-independent in the exact GP, an information bottleneck because the finite-dimensional representation cannot resolve the full context geometry, and amortization error from a single encoder network shared across all contexts. The bottleneck truncation term decays in the representation dimension $d$ as $O(e^{-cd^{2/d_x}})$ for squared-exponential kernels on $\mathbb{R}^{d_x}$ where $c > 0$ is a kernel-dependent constant and as $O(d^{-2ν/d_x})$ for Matérn-$ν$ kernels, directly linking architecture sizing to kernel smoothness and input dimension. The label contamination term is $O(1)$ in general, with only the observation-noise component decaying as $O(1/n)$, identifying a persistent cost of routing uncertainty estimation through a label-dependent representation. These results characterize the costs of amortization within the analyzed class and yield architectural recommendations to predict variance from context locations alone in the GP-amortization regime, and replace mean aggregation with second-order pooling to close the dominant amortization gap.

</details>


### [193] [stable-worldmodel: A Platform for Reproducible World Modeling Research and Evaluation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21800)
*Lucas Maes,Quentin Le Lidec,Luiz Facury,Nassim Massaudi,Ayush Chaurasia,Francesco Capuano,Richard Gao,Taj Gillin,Dan Haramati,Damien Scieur,Yann LeCun,Randall Balestriero*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前世界模型研究存在代码库分散、数据管道不一致、评估协议各异等问题，导致研究难以复现和公平比较；同时面临一次性代码脆弱、视频数据加载缓慢、缺乏标准化泛化基准三大瓶颈，阻碍了可靠世界模型的发展。

Method: 开发了一个基于Lance的数据层，原生支持MP4、HDF5和LeRobot数据格式，并提供转换工具；整合现代世界模型基线与规划求解器的干净、可测试实现；构建包含可控视觉、几何与物理因素的多样化环境与任务，支持系统性仿真评估。

Result: swm平台显著降低了研究开销，提升了实验可复现性，加速了对动态理解、控制性能、表征质量及分布外泛化能力的可信评估，推动世界模型研究向更高效、标准化的方向发展。

Conclusion: 通过统一数据、模型与评估全流程，swm为世界模型研究提供了标准化、可扩展、高性能的基础设施，是实现可靠、可比较世界模型研究的关键一步。

Abstract: World models are central to building agents that can reason, plan, and generalize beyond their training data. However, research on world models is currently fragmented, with disparate codebases, data pipelines, and evaluation protocols hindering reproducibility and fair comparison. Current practice is further limited by three key bottlenecks: fragile one-off codebases, slow video data loading, and the lack of standardized generalization benchmarks. We present stable-worldmodel (swm), an open-source platform for standardized and reproducible world modeling research and evaluation. It delivers (1) a high-performance Lance-based data layer with native support and conversion tools for MP4, HDF5, and LeRobot datasets, (2) clean, well-tested implementations of modern world model baselines and planning solvers, and (3) a broad suite of environments and tasks extended with controllable visual, geometric, and physical factors of variation for systematic in-silico evaluation of dynamics understanding, control performance, representation quality, and out-of-distribution generalization. By unifying the full pipeline under a single, scalable framework, \texttt{swm} dramatically reduces research overhead and accelerates trustworthy progress toward reliable world models.

Motivation: 现有后训练方法缺乏有效的机制来区分信息性信号与噪声信号，且基于熵的估计器存在各向异性偏差和校准偏差问题，导致优化动态不稳定。

Method: 提出几何感知校准策略（GCPO），结合语义分歧的几何感知测量与奖励驱动的校准，以对齐不确定性信号与学习信号强度。

Result: 在多个基准测试中，该方法能更准确地跟踪梯度变异性，并显著提升后训练性能，表现出更强的鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 设计与优化动态对齐的不确定性信号至关重要，本工作为稳健后训练提供了理论指导和实践框架。

Abstract: Post-training has become central to improving reasoning and alignment in large language models, where critic-free models enable scalable learning from model-generated outputs but lack principled mechanisms to distinguish informative from noisy signals. Recent approaches leverage response-level measures as uncertainty signals to regulate group-based optimization methods such as GRPO. Yet their empirical success remains unstable and unclear in how they influence optimization dynamics. In this paper, we provide, to our knowledge, the first principled formulation that interprets uncertainty signals as mechanisms for characterizing and regulating gradient variance and learning signal quality. Based on both empirical and theoretical analysis, we identify two critical gaps of current entropy-based estimators: The anisotropic gap and The calibration gap. Motivated by this analysis, we propose Geometric-aware Calibrated Policy Optimization (GCPO), a novel framework integrating geometry-aware measures to capture semantic disagreement with reward-based calibration to align uncertainty with learning signal strength. Experiments on multiple benchmarks show that our approach more faithfully tracks gradient variability and consistently improves post-training performance. Our results highlight the importance of designing uncertainty signals that are aligned with optimization dynamics, offering a principled perspective for robust post-training.

Existing consistency training procedures generate the supervision signal once, offline, and use supervised fine-tuning (SFT) to update the model. Unfortunately, the resulting models tend to merely memorize the surface forms of the training distribution and thus generalize poorly and regress in their capabilities. We introduce On-Policy Consistency Training (OPCT), a new consistency training approach where the objective is computed over the model's own responses to prompts, supervised by itself conditioned on corresponding contrastive prompts. We evaluate OPCT on three safety axes: sycophancy, jailbreaking, and safety awareness. Across three model families, OPCT outperforms its SFT counterpart on all safety desiderata. Our results suggest that consistency training is best implemented as OPCT rather than as SFT, especially when generalization beyond the training distribution is desired.

### [198] [Energy-Gated Attention: Spectral Salience as an Inductive Bias for Transformer Attention](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21842)
*Athanasios Zeris*

Main category: cs.LG

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准Transformer注意力对所有词元同等对待，忽视其内在信息量差异；类比湍流中相干结构集中能量，提出词元的信息密度应决定其注意力权重。

Method: 引入线性投影计算词元嵌入的谱能量，通过学习得到的能量阈值门控值聚合，实现信息密集词元的优先关注。

Result: 在TinyShakespeare上验证损失降低0.103，Penn Treebank上降低0.101，参数增加不足0.26%，计算成本不变；能量阈值稳定收敛至0.35，符合语言学规律。

Conclusion: EGA有效提升了注意力机制对关键信息的捕捉能力，揭示了语言中信息分布的稳定性，并指出数据自适应的非正弦谱基是未来方向。

Abstract: Standard transformer attention computes pairwise similarity between queries and keys, treating all tokens as equally salient regardless of their intrinsic informational content. In turbulent fluid dynamics, coherent structures -- the energetically dominant, spatially organized patterns that persist amid background chaos -- carry a disproportionate fraction of total energy and govern all transport. We propose that tokens play an analogous role in transformer attention: informationally dense positions (morphological boundaries, syntactic heads, discourse markers) concentrate spectral energy and should attract proportionally more attention than background tokens (function words, repeated patterns, low-information filler). We propose Energy-Gated Attention (EGA): a simple modification that gates value aggregation by the spectral energy of key token embeddings, computed by a single learned linear projection that discovers the dominant spectral mode of the embedding field. On TinyShakespeare, EGA achieves +0.103 validation loss improvement with only 12,480 additional parameters (<0.26% overhead) and no measurable computational cost. The result is consistent on Penn Treebank (+0.101), demonstrating dataset independence. A systematic ablation across three wavelet families (fixed Morlet, Daubechies db2/db4, and a parametric Morlet) establishes that fixed structured bases are suboptimal -- the optimal energy direction is data-adaptive and non-sinusoidal -- while identifying learned wavelet packets as a promising open direction. The learned energy threshold converges to tau ~= 0.35 independently of initialization, corresponding to the fraction (~36%) of tokens carrying above-average spectral energy in English text, a stable linguistic property consistent with the fraction of content words in running English text.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有字典类解释器（如稀疏自编码器、转换器）在分布外（OOD）场景下的忠实度缺乏系统研究，而实际应用中模型常面临分布偏移，导致解释失效。因此亟需理解并缓解这一问题。

Method: 提出几何自适应解释器（GAE），通过分析分布偏移引起的子空间旋转，利用无标签的OOD激活数据，对解释器字典进行几何调整以重新对齐到新的活跃子空间，保持原始特征结构的同时提升对OOD的解释能力。

Abstract: Mechanistic interpretability aims to explain a model's behavior by identifying causally responsible internal structures. Dictionary-based explainers such as sparse autoencoders and transcoders are a primary tool, but their faithfulness under out-of-distribution (OOD) shift has received little systematic attention. We show that distribution shift rotates the subspace that the model actively uses, misaligning the explainer's dictionary trained on in-distribution (ID) activations. We formalize this misalignment as the faithfulness gap, a geometric distance between the ID dictionary and the OOD-active subspace, and show that it controls OOD faithfulness degradation. To reduce this gap, we propose the Geometry-Adaptive Explainer (GAE), which realigns the explainer's dictionary with the OOD-active subspace while preserving the original feature structure. This requires only unlabeled OOD activations and no gradient updates. We prove that GAE improves over the unadapted ID explainer, with excess loss bounded quadratically by the second-moment shift. Empirically, GAE even matches or surpasses all training-based baselines in causal faithfulness across multiple models and OOD settings.

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) have demonstrated impressive reasoning abilities across a wide range of tasks, but data contamination undermines the objective evaluation of these capabilities. This problem is further exacerbated by malicious model publishers who use evasive, or indirect, contamination strategies, such as paraphrasing benchmark data to evade existing detection methods and artificially boost leaderboard performance. Current approaches struggle to reliably detect such stealthy contamination. In this work, we uncover a critical phenomenon: a model's generated reasoning steps actively mask its underlying memorization. Inspired by this, we propose the Zero-CoT Probe (ZCP), a novel black-box detection method that deliberately truncates the entire Chain-of-Thought (CoT) process to expose latent shortcut mappings. To further isolate memorization from the model's intrinsic problem-solving capabilities, ZCP compares the model's zero-CoT performance on the original benchmark against an isomorphically perturbed reference dataset. Furthermore, we introduce Contamination Confidence, a metric that quantifies both the likelihood and severity of contamination, moving beyond simple binary classifications. Extensive experiments on both previously identified contaminated models and specially fine-tuned contaminated models demonstrate that ZCP robustly detects both direct and evasive data contamination. ### [201] [When to Switch, Not Just What: Transition Quality Prediction in Clash Royale](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21868)
*Heeyun Heo,Huy Kang Kim*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究分析了92万多场Clash Royale比赛数据，发现玩家在连败后频繁换策略反而与较低胜率相关。作者指出，传统推荐系统假设切换策略无成本（零切换成本假设），忽视了切换行为本身带来的代价及个体差异。为此提出TQP框架，包含三阶段：谁（PersonaGate）、何时（TimingGate）、如何（ScoreFusion），通过识别适合稳定策略的玩家、判断切换时机、结合可采纳性与胜率变化预测推荐最优策略。引入SwitchGap评估指标，避免将玩家实际选择视为最优。最终模型在5.4%推荐率下提升10.4个百分点的区分度，连败者受益最大。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有推荐系统通常基于策略的预期质量进行评估，但忽略了策略切换的行为成本以及玩家个体差异，导致推荐策略与实际表现不匹配。尤其在连败后频繁换策略的玩家中，虽行为频繁但胜率最低，说明当前方法存在根本缺陷。因此需要重新建模策略推荐问题，考虑切换的代价和个体特性。

Method: 提出TQP（Transition Quality Predictor）三阶段框架：1）PersonaGate识别策略一致性与高胜率相关的玩家，抑制对其推荐；2）TimingGate通过子类型和状态匹配的基线，识别切换可能带来净收益的时机；3）ScoreFusion结合采纳信号与预测的胜率变化（delta WR）对候选策略排序。引入SwitchGap作为新评估指标，衡量政策的判别能力而不依赖玩家真实选择为最优。

Result: TQP框架在5.4%推荐率下实现+10.4个百分点的SwitchGap提升，显著优于基准。连败触发切换的玩家群体尽管整体表现最差，却从子类型条件化指导中获益最大，验证了个性化推荐的有效性。

Conclusion: 传统的策略推荐忽视切换成本和个体差异，导致无效甚至有害建议。TQP框架通过精细化建模切换行为，在真实场景中显著提升了推荐效果，尤其对低绩效玩家具有重要价值。研究揭示了‘零切换成本假设’的局限性，并为游戏推荐系统提供了可推广的新范式。

Abstract: In competitive games, players frequently switch strategies after losing streaks, yet our analysis of 926,334 match records from 34,619 Clash Royale players reveals a counterintuitive pattern: switching frequency is inversely associated with the win rate, with effects that vary substantially across players and situational contexts. We attribute this to a limitation common in many prior recommendation systems, which evaluate strategies by expected quality while overlooking the behavioral cost of switching and individual differences in switching propensity. We refer to this implicit premise as the Zero Switching Cost Assumption. To address this, we reformulate strategy recommendation as a transition-level decision problem and instantiate it as TQP (Transition Quality Predictor), a three-stage pipeline structured as Who -> When -> What. PersonaGate suppresses recommendations for players whose strategic consistency is empirically associated with superior outcomes. TimingGate identifies moments when switching is likely to yield a net benefit over staying, using a subtype- and state-matched baseline to control for natural win-rate recovery. ScoreFusion ranks candidate strategies by combining an adoptability signal with predicted transition quality (delta WR). We further introduce SwitchGap, an evaluation metric that measures a policy's discriminative quality without treating observed player choices as optimal ground truth. This property is particularly important because the most frequent switchers record the lowest win rates. The full pipeline achieves a SwitchGap of +10.4 percentage points at a recommendation rate of 5.4%, and loss-triggered switchers, despite being the lowest-performing group, benefit the most from subtype-conditioned guidance.

</details>


### [202] [Noise Schedule Design for Diffusion Models: An Optimal Control Perspective](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21911)
*Seo Taek Kong,Weina Wang,R. Srikant*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一个原则性框架，用于分析和设计扩散模型中的噪声调度。通过将噪声调度设计问题转化为最优控制问题，其中状态为扩散过程的Fisher信息，控制输入为噪声调度，目标函数是关于Fisher信息的泛函，该泛函为KL采样误差的上界。通过求解此最优控制问题，推导出实现当前最优$\tilde{\mathcal{O}}(d/n)$采样误差的充分条件。在数据分布的参数化假设下，可获得噪声调度的闭式表达式，这些调度推广了常用的指数和S型调度，并引入可调参数以优化性能。系统调节这些参数可得到新调度，在图像生成基准上取得更优的FID分数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有理论工作虽证明$\tilde{\mathcal{O}}(d/n)$采样误差可达，但仅针对特定噪声调度，不涵盖实际中使用的调度。因此需要建立一个通用框架，既能保证理论性能，又能指导实际调度设计。

Method: 将噪声调度设计问题建模为最优控制问题，状态变量为扩散过程的Fisher信息，控制变量为噪声调度，目标函数为基于Fisher信息的泛函，用以最小化采样误差上界。通过求解该最优控制问题，推导出满足$\tilde{\mathcal{O}}(d/n)$误差的充分条件，并在参数化假设下获得闭式噪声调度表达式。

Result: 推导出实现$\tilde{\mathcal{O}}(d/n)$采样误差的噪声调度充分条件；在参数化假设下，获得可调参数的闭式噪声调度，实验表明其在图像生成任务中优于标准调度，显著提升FID得分。

Conclusion: 本文提出的最优控制框架为扩散模型的噪声调度设计提供了理论依据与实用工具，所推导的可调噪声调度在理论上保证性能，并在实践中显著提升生成质量。

Abstract: We develop a principled framework for analyzing and designing noise schedules in diffusion models. We show that one can recast this design problem as an optimal control problem, whose state is the Fisher information of the diffusion process which evolves according to an ODE and the control input is the noise schedule. The objective of the optimal control problem is a functional involving the Fisher information, which is shown to be an upper bound on the Kullback-Leibler sampling error. By solving this optimal control problem, we obtain sufficient conditions on noise schedules under which state-of-the-art $\tilde{\mathcal{O}} (d/n)$ sampling error is achievable, where $d$ is the data dimension and $n$ is the number of discretization steps. While existing theoretical work also prove that $\tilde{\mathcal{O}}(d/n)$ sampling error bounds are achievable, these results hold for specific noise schedules, which do not include the schedules used in practice. Under a further parametric assumption on the data distribution, we show that one can obtain closed-form expressions for the noise schedules. These noise schedules generalize standard empirical schedules such as exponential and sigmoid schedules by allowing additional parameters that can be tuned. Systematically tuning the parameters of these schedules yields new schedules that achieve superior FID scores on image generation benchmarks.

</details>


### [203] [CausalGuard: Conformal Inference under Graph Uncertainty](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21928)
*Vikash Singh,Weicong Chen,Debargha Ganguly,Yanyan Zhang,Nengbo Wang,Sreehari Sankar,Mohsen Hariri,Alexander Nemecek,Chaoda Song,Shouren Wang,Biyao Zhang,Van Yang,Erman Ayday,Jing Ma,Vipin Chaudhary*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: CausalGuard 是一种结构加权的置信区间框架，通过整合基于大语言模型（LLM）生成的边先验、条件独立性检验剪枝和贝叶斯信息准则重加权的候选因果图，构建复合非符合性得分，实现对双重稳健伪结果的校准。该方法在有限样本下提供分布无关的边际覆盖，且在因果可识别、重叠性、条件均值扰动稳定性和目标对齐有效调整策略集中时，其条件均值收敛于真实的条件平均处理效应。在五个基准测试中，CausalGuard 在直接可评估目标上实现了超过90%名义覆盖率，并在图无关置信区间基线需大幅填充时显著缩小区间宽度。压力测试表明，该方法能抑制无效共因调整，即使在先验错误的情况下仍保持稳定性，前提是保留的候选集由数据支持。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在观察性数据中估计处理效应需要选择合适的调整集，但有效调整依赖于未知的因果图。若因果图误设会导致覆盖不足；而图无关的置信包装方法虽可恢复名义覆盖，但往往需大量填充才能实现。因此，亟需一种既能保证覆盖性又具备高效性的方法。

Method: 提出 CausalGuard 框架：1）利用大语言模型生成初始边先验；2）通过条件独立性检验剪枝候选有向无环图（DAG）；3）使用贝叶斯信息准则对候选图进行重加权；4）聚合图条件下的双重稳健伪结果；5）构造后验加权的复合非符合性得分进行置信区间校准。

Result: CausalGuard 在有限样本下提供分布无关的边际覆盖；在满足因果可识别性、重叠性、条件均值扰动稳定性以及目标对齐的有效调整策略集中时，其条件均值收敛于真实 CATE；在五项基准测试中，平均覆盖率达90%以上，且相比图无关基线显著减小置信区间宽度；在先验错误但候选集由数据支持时仍保持稳定，有效抑制无效共因调整。

Conclusion: CausalGuard 通过融合因果结构学习与置信区间校准，实现了高覆盖率与紧凑区间的平衡，尤其适用于因果图不确定场景，是当前图敏感与图无关方法之间的一种有效折中。

Abstract: Estimating treatment effects from observational data requires choosing an adjustment set, but valid adjustment depends on an unknown causal graph. Graph misspecification can cause under-coverage, while graph-agnostic conformal wrappers may regain nominal coverage only through large padding. We introduce CausalGuard, a structure-weighted conformal framework that calibrates after aggregating graph-conditional doubly robust pseudo-outcomes. Candidate DAGs are proposed from an LLM-derived edge prior, pruned by conditional-independence tests, and reweighted by Bayesian Information Criterion. A composite nonconformity score then calibrates the posterior-weighted pseudo-outcome. CausalGuard provides distribution-free finite-sample marginal coverage for this aggregated pseudo-outcome; under causal identification, overlap, conditional-mean nuisance stability, and concentration on target-aligned valid adjustment strategies, its conditional mean converges to the true Conditional Average Treatment Effect. Across five benchmarks, CausalGuard attains mean coverage above the nominal 90% level for the directly evaluable target and reduces width when graph-agnostic conformal baselines require large padding. Stress tests show that CausalGuard suppresses invalid collider adjustment and remains stable under misspecified priors when the retained candidate set is data-supported.

### [204] [Optimal Guarantees for Auditing Rényi Differentially Private Machine Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21938)
*Benjamin D. Kim,Lav R. Varshney,Daniel Alabi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于假设检验的黑盒审计框架，用于评估声称满足瑞尼差分隐私（RDP）的机器学习算法。该框架利用Donsker-Varadhan（DV）变分估计器直接估算相邻执行之间的瑞尼散度，并提供了非渐近的置信区间，将统计估计误差与算法隐私泄露分离。研究证明了匹配的极小极大下界，表明在对数因子范围内，样本复杂度保证是信息论最优的，首次实现了基于DV估计器的RDP审计的最优性。实验上，该框架在完全黑盒设置下应用于审计DP-SGD，在MNIST和CIFAR-10数据集上，相较于现有最先进方法，在小到中等瑞尼阶数下显著提升了经验RDP下界估计的准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的黑盒审计方法在小和中等瑞尼阶数下难以准确评估机器学习模型的隐私保护能力，尤其是在缺乏内部机制信息的情况下。因此需要一种更精确、理论上最优且可实用的审计框架来验证模型是否真正满足瑞尼差分隐私。

Method: 提出基于假设检验的审计框架，使用Donsker-Varadhan（DV）变分估计器直接估计相邻执行间的瑞尼散度；通过类限制的DV估计器构建非渐近置信区间，分离统计误差与隐私泄漏；并建立极小极大下界以证明样本复杂度的最优性。

Result: 所提框架在多个数据集（如MNIST和CIFAR-10）和不同隐私配置下，显著优于现有黑盒审计方法，尤其在小和中等瑞尼阶数时表现突出；同时理论证明其样本复杂度接近信息论最优。

Conclusion: 本文提出的审计框架首次实现了基于DV估计器的瑞尼差分隐私审计的信息论最优性，并在实际应用中展现出显著优越性，为黑盒环境下隐私保障提供了强有力的工具。

Abstract: We study black-box auditing for machine learning algorithms that claim R \ 'enyi differential privacy (RDP) guarantees. We introduce an auditing framework, based on hypothesis testing, that directly estimates Rényi divergence between neighboring executions using the Donsker-Varadhan (DV) variational estimator. Our analysis yields explicit and non-asymptotic confidence intervals for RDP auditing via class-restricted DV estimators, separating statistical estimation error from algorithmic privacy leakage. We prove matching minimax lower bounds showing that, up to logarithmic factors, our sample-complexity guarantees are information-theoretically optimal, thereby establishing the first optimal guarantees for auditing RDP via DV estimators. Empirically, we instantiate our framework for auditing DP-SGD in a fully black-box setting. Across MNIST and CIFAR-10, and over a wide range of privacy regimes, our auditors produce a strong overall improvement on empirical RDP lower bounds compared to prior state-of-the-art black-box methods especially at small and moderate Rényi orders where accurate auditing is most challenging.

### [205] [SCI-Defense: Defending Manipulation Attacks from Generative Engine Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21948)
*Xucheng Yu,Haibo Jin,Huimin Zeng,Haohan Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: SCI-Defense 是一种针对大语言模型排名系统中生成引擎优化（GEO）攻击的三组件防御框架，结合了困惑度检测（PPL）、语义完整性评分（SIS）和候选间检测（ICD）。SIS 评估权威归属、叙事目的性、比较性陈述和时间性陈述四个维度。在亚马逊600个产品描述上测试，对字符串、推理和评论攻击分别达到1.000、0.952和0.830的召回率，且精确率1.000，假阳性率0.000。在MS MARCO网页片段上，字符串攻击可被完全阻止，但评论攻击召回率接近零，因网页缺乏产品描述中的说服性信号。现有方法如仅用PPL、SafetyClf或改写均无法应对语义操纵攻击。新攻击如规格放大和使用场景饱和暴露了当前结构化防御的盲点，指明未来研究方向。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型驱动的排名系统易受生成引擎优化（GEO）攻击，攻击者通过向产品描述中注入语义信号来人为提升排名，亟需有效防御机制。

Method: 提出SCI-Defense框架，包含三个组件：困惑度检测（PPL）、语义完整性评分（SIS）和候选间检测（ICD）。SIS从权威归属、叙事目的性、比较性陈述和时间性陈述四个维度评估文本语义完整性。

Result: 在亚马逊600个产品描述上，SCI-Defense实现精确率1.000、假阳性率0.000，对字符串、推理和评论攻击的召回率分别为1.000、0.952和0.830。在MS MARCO数据集上，字符串攻击可被完全阻断，而评论攻击召回率趋近于零。现有方法（PPL-only、SafetyClf、 paraphrasing）对语义操纵攻击召回率为零。新攻击揭示了当前结构化防御的盲点。

Conclusion: SCI-Defense在对抗语义操纵攻击方面表现出色，但现有防御体系仍存在结构性盲点。新攻击类型表明，未来需探索更鲁棒的防御机制以应对复杂语义操纵。

Abstract: LLM-based ranking systems are vulnerable to Generative Engine Optimization (GEO) attacks, where adversaries inject semantic signals into product descriptions to artificially boost rankings. We propose SCI-Defense, a three-component defense framework combining Perplexity detection (PPL), Semantic Integrity Scoring (SIS), and Inter-Candidate Detection (ICD). SIS evaluates four manipulation dimensions: Authority Attribution (AA), Narrative Purposiveness (NP), Comparative Claims (CA), and Temporal Claims (TC). Evaluated on 600 Amazon product descriptions across 6 categories, SCI-Defense achieves Precision=1.000 and FPR=0.000, with Recall of 1.000, 0.952, and 0.830 against String, Reasoning, and Review attacks respectively. On 600 MS MARCO web passages, String attacks are blocked with perfect recall while Review attacks yield near-zero recall, as web passages lack the persuasion-oriented signals that SIS targets in product descriptions. We demonstrate that existing defenses -- PPL-only filters, SafetyClf content classifiers, and paraphrasing -- achieve zero recall against semantic manipulation attacks. We further demonstrate new attacks such as Specification Amplification and Use-Case Saturation can expose semantic relevance manipulation as a structural defense blind spot that suggests directions for future research.

### [206] [Dynamic Mixture of Latent Memories for Self-Evolving Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21951)
*Dianzhi Yu,Vireo Zhang,Hongru Wang,Yanyu Chen,Minda Hu,Wanghan Xu,Siki Chen,Philip Torr,Zhenfei Yin,Irwin King*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: MoLEM提出一种基于动态专家混合（MoE）的生成式潜在记忆框架，通过独立专家生成记忆，利用路由器根据键值匹配选择并加权专家，将聚合的潜在记忆注入推理过程。基础模型保持冻结，所有经验知识内化到额外模块中，避免灾难性遗忘。在持续学习中，每个训练阶段配有一个轻量级自编码器，用于推理时选择合适的路由组，不匹配任何阶段的输入则回退到预训练模型。实验在数学、科学和代码领域连续学习序列上进行，结果表明，经过完整连续学习序列后，该方法相比基线模型平均准确率提升10.40%，且无其他方法能在不同训练顺序下始终超越基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法在智能体自我进化中面临知识遗忘问题：参数更新导致灾难性遗忘，外部记忆无法真正增强模型内在能力。需要一种既能持续积累新知识又不丢失旧能力的方法。

Result: 在跨数学、科学、代码领域的连续学习任务中，MoLEM在完成全部训练后，平均准确率比基线模型高出10.40%；且在不同训练顺序下，无其他方法能持续超越该基线。

Conclusion: MoLEM成功实现了智能体在持续学习中的知识积累与能力保留，通过外部记忆模块实现无遗忘的知识内化，为智能体的自我演化提供了有效解决方案。

Abstract: Achieving self-evolution in intelligent agents requires the continual accumulation of new knowledge across changing task sequences without forgetting previously acquired abilities. Existing approaches either internalize knowledge by updating model parameters, which induces catastrophic forgetting, or rely on external memory, which fails to genuinely enhance the model's intrinsic capabilities. We propose MoLEM, a generative mixture of latent memory framework based on a dynamic mixture-of-experts (MoE). We treat multiple experts as independent carriers to generate memory. A router selects and weights experts through key-query matching, and the aggregated latent memory is injected into the reasoning process. The base model for reasoning remains entirely frozen, with all experiential knowledge internalized into the additional modules, avoiding catastrophic forgetting. For continual learning, each training stage is paired with a lightweight autoencoder that selects the appropriate routing group at inference, and inputs that match no stage fall back to the pretrained model. Experiments train the framework on continual-learning sequences spanning math, science, and code domains. After training, we evaluate the framework on the corresponding test sets to measure task learning and competence preservation across continual adaptation stages. After the full continual-learning sequence, our method improves the average accuracy by 10.40% over the Vanilla pretrained baseline, while none of the competing methods consistently exceed this baseline across different training orders.

### [207] [ChronoMedicalWorld: A Medical World Model for Learning Patient Trajectories from Longitudinal Care Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21963)

Abstract: Long-horizon clinical simulation -- predicting how a patient's physiology evolves over years under specified interventions -- is central to chronic-disease care, yet existing electronic health record (EHR) models are predominantly discriminative, and general-purpose large language models drift under repeated interventions. We propose the \textbf{ChronoMedicalWorld Model (CMWM)}, an action-conditioned latent world-model framework for learning patient trajectories from longitudinal care data. CMWM couples a joint-embedding state encoder with a wide action encoder that admits both structured intervention indicators and free-text communication embeddings, and trains a recurrent latent transition module under a six-term objective: next-observation supervision, next-latent prediction, SIGReg latent regularisation, and three physiology-aware shape priors (slope, continuity, large-jump penalty). A closed-loop rollout-prefix protocol matches training to deployment, so the model is optimised against the same multi-step error it exhibits at inference. As a concrete case study, we instantiate CMWM for annual estimated glomerular filtration rate (eGFR) trajectory forecasting in chronic kidney disease (CKD). On a 2{,}232-patient nephrology cohort, the CKD instantiation achieves a dynamic-50\% history rollout test mean absolute error (MAE) of 7.384 and root-mean-square error (RMSE) of 10.256, against 7.964 and 11.069 for a tuned GPT-5.5 structured-prompting baseline ($-7.28\%$ MAE, $-7.35\%$ RMSE), with the gain dominated by the dialogue portion of patient--health-coach communication. The framework is not CKD-specific: its architecture, loss design, and training protocol apply to any chronic condition that can be cast as periodic clinical state interleaved with structured and conversational interventions.

Abstract: Optimization is essential in deep learning. The foundational method upon which most optimizers are built is momentum-based stochastic gradient descent. However, it suffers from two key drawbacks. First, it has noisy and varying gradients, and second, it has an overshoot phenomenon. To address noisy gradients, Adam was proposed, which remains the most widely used adaptive optimizer. To address the overshoot phenomenon, a control-theory-based PID optimizer was proposed. To tackle both the limitations within a single framework, several variants of Adaptive PID (AdaPID) have recently been proposed.
  Although AdaPID performs well, it still inherits two critical drawbacks from Adam, namely convergence and stability issues. In this work, we address both these limitations. To fix the convergence issue, we uniquely integrate the idea of using a non-increasing effective learning rate into AdaPID (originally proposed in AMSGrad, an extension of Adam). To fix the stability issue, we innovatively integrate a gradient difference based modulation factor into AdaPID (originally proposed in DiffGrad, another extension of Adam). Combining both these ideas in AdaPID, results in our novel IAdaPID-ADG optimizer.
  We evaluate our proposed optimizer on multiple datasets, including benchmark datasets (MNIST and CIFAR10) and real-world datasets (IARC and AnnoCerv). The IAdaPID-ADG substantially outperforms all competing optimizers. Additionally, we perform an ablation study on the MNIST dataset to demonstrate the contribution of each added component.

</details>


### [209] [Reasoning through Verifiable Forecast Actions: Consistency-Grounded RL for Financial LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21975)
*Jialin Chen,Aosong Feng,Harshit Verma,Siyi Gu,Haiwen Wang,Ali Maatouk,Yixuan He,Yifeng Gao,Leandros Tassiulas,Rex Ying*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: StockR1 是一种时间序列增强型大语言模型，通过可验证的预测动作统一股票预测与金融推理。该模型采用工具调用设计，先生成结构化、可解释的定性市场展望（预测动作），再基于此动作调用时间序列解码器生成分布式的未来走势轨迹，实现定量与定性推理的融合。通过强化学习优化整个流程，奖励机制结合答案有效性、预测准确性和动作与实际时间序列动态的一致性，并引入样本级不确定性权重以适应市场波动性。在大规模10年基准上评估，StockR1显著优于时序基线和通用大模型，推理准确率提升17.7%（4B）和25.9%（8B），证明了结构化预测动作能有效促进语言推理与时间预测之间的协同作用，使大模型能够做出可验证、可解释且数值依据充分的决策。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法要么将时间序列抽象为文本，要么将预测与基于语言的推理分离，导致定性分析与定量结果之间存在根本性脱节。金融市场的非平稳性、低信噪比及对外部信息的高度依赖使得这种脱节更加严重，亟需一种能融合语言推理与时间序列预测的统一框架。

Method: 提出StockR1模型，采用工具调用架构：首先生成结构化的预测动作（代表定性市场观点），然后利用条件于该动作的时间序列解码器生成未来价格分布轨迹；整个系统通过强化学习进行端到端优化，奖励函数综合考虑答案正确性、预测精度以及预测动作与真实时间序列动态的一致性，并引入样本级不确定性权重以增强对市场不确定性的适应能力。

Result: 在10年大规模金融问答与股票预测基准上，StockR1显著优于主流时间序列模型和通用大语言模型，在4B和8B参数量下分别实现17.7%和25.9%的推理准确率提升，验证了其在融合语言推理与时间预测方面的优越性。

Conclusion: 通过结构化预测动作建立语言推理与时间序列预测之间的强耦合，StockR1实现了可验证、可解释且数值可信的金融决策，为大模型在复杂金融场景中的应用提供了新范式。

Abstract: Financial markets are characterized by extreme non-stationarity, low signal-to-noise ratios, and strong dependence on external information such as news, company fundamentals, and macroeconomic signals. Yet, existing approaches either abstract time-series into text or decouple forecasting from language-based reasoning, leading to a fundamental mismatch between qualitative reasoning and quantitative outcomes. To address this, we introduce StockR1, a time-series-enhanced LLM that unifies stock forecasting and financial reasoning through a verifiable forecast action. Based on a tool-call design, the model first emits a forecast action, which is a structured and interpretable representation of its qualitative market outlook. It then invokes a time-series decoder conditioned on this action to generate distributional future trajectories, leading to more informed question answering and financial reasoning. We optimize the full pipeline with reinforcement learning, where rewards jointly reflect answer validity, forecast accuracy, and consistency between generated actions and observed time-series dynamics. In addition, rewards are reweighted by a sample-level uncertainty scalar, encouraging the model to accommodate varying uncertainty in market dynamics. We evaluate StockR1 on financial question answering and stock forecasting over a large-scale 10-year benchmark. Our method consistently outperforms time-series baselines and general-purpose LLMs, improving reasoning accuracy by 17.7% (4B) and 25.9% (8B). These findings demonstrate that structuring the forecast actions establishes a powerful synergy between language reasoning and temporal prediction, enabling LLMs to reason through verifiable, interpretable, and numerically grounded decisions.

### [210] [Ex-GraphRAG: Interpretable Evidence Routing for Graph-Augmented LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21994)
*Yoav Kor Sade,Arvindh Arun,Rishi Puri,Steffen Staab,Maya Bechler-Speicher*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: Ex-GraphRAG replaces GNN encoders with M-GNAN to enable exact attribution of node contributions in graph-augmented LLMs, revealing a semantic-structural mismatch where key nodes are structurally disconnected yet crucial for reasoning.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Existing GNN-based encoders in GraphRAG entangle node contributions through neighborhood aggregation, making it impossible to determine individual node influence, thus hindering auditability and interpretability of evidence routing.

Method: Introduces Multivariate Graph Neural Additive Network (M-GNAN), an additive model extension to high-dimensional embeddings that provides exact decomposition of encoder output across nodes and feature groups without approximation.

Result: On STaRK-Prime, Ex-GraphRAG matches black-box performance while enabling precise auditing; reveals that dominant nodes in outputs are structurally disconnected, relying on low-attribution intermediaries whose removal degrades multi-hop QA by up to 28%.

Conclusion: Semantic importance and structural connectivity are governed by disjoint node sets, exposing critical limitations in retrieval pruning and context construction, and highlighting the need for interpretable, auditable encoders in graph-augmented LLMs.

Abstract: GraphRAG conditions language models on subgraphs retrieved from knowledge graphs, encoded via message-passing GNNs. Because these encoders entangle node contributions through iterated neighborhood aggregation, there is no closed-form way to determine how much each retrieved entity influenced the encoder's output, and therefore no way to faithfully audit what structural evidence actually reached the model. We introduce Ex-GraphRAG, which replaces the GNN encoder with a Multivariate Graph Neural Additive Network (M-GNAN), an extension of additive graph models to high-dimensional embedding spaces that yields an exact decomposition of the encoder's output across individual nodes and feature groups, without post-hoc approximation. On STaRK-Prime, this auditable encoder matches black-box performance. Using it to audit evidence routing, we uncover a semantic-structural mismatch: the nodes that dominate the encoder's output are structurally disconnected in the retrieved subgraph, held together by low-attribution intermediaries whose removal degrades multi-hop QA by up to 28%. This mismatch, invisible to any opaque encoder, reveals that semantic importance and structural connectivity are governed by disjoint sets of nodes, with direct implications for retrieval pruning, context construction, and failure diagnosis in graph-augmented LLMs.

</details>


### [211] [Check Your LLM's Secret Dictionary! Five Lines of Code Reveal What Your LLM Learned (Including What It Shouldn't Have)](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22005)
*Hisashi Miyashita*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 通过分析Transformer语言模型lm_head权重矩阵的奇异值分解（SVD），仅用五行PyTorch代码即可揭示可解释的语义子空间，无需模型推理。该方法能暴露模型训练数据组成与数据筛选理念。在GPT-OSS-120B、Gemma-2-2B和Qwen2.5-1.5B上的实验显示，不同模型具有系统性差异：GPT呈现功能分层的子空间结构；Gemma受19世纪前英语拼写主导，形成阶梯式聚类，可能提升输出可控性；Qwen则展现广泛多语言覆盖，但存在伦理问题词汇子空间。对比base与instruct版本发现，问题内容源于预训练阶段，后训练对齐无法消除。提出VCS量化子空间一致性，WPS作为静态幻觉词检测工具，成功在不进行推理的情况下识别出知名中文幻觉词shokubutsu-hyakka-tsu（ID 137606）。研究建议将lm_head SVD分析纳入模型发布前的安全审计标准，并为基于SVD的分词器优化与更可控的LLM设计提供方向。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 揭示大型语言模型内部语义结构，理解其训练数据组成与潜在伦理风险，提出一种无需模型推理的高效安全审计方法，以提升模型透明度与可控性。

Method: 对lm_head权重矩阵进行奇异值分解（SVD），分析左奇异向量对应的词汇簇，评估子空间结构与一致性，引入VCS和WPS指标进行量化分析，并结合案例验证其有效性。

Result: 不同模型表现出显著不同的子空间结构：GPT具有功能分层特征，Gemma体现历史拼写主导，Qwen包含多语言与伦理问题词汇。问题子空间源自预训练阶段，且可通过WPS有效检测幻觉词如shokubutsu-hyakka-tsu。SVD分析可作为有效的静态安全审计手段。

Conclusion: lm_head的SVD分析是一种强大、轻量且高效的模型分析工具，可用于揭示模型语义结构、识别伦理风险、检测幻觉词，并应被采纳为模型发布前的标准安全审计流程。同时，该方法为分词器优化与更可控的模型设计提供了新思路。

Abstract: We show that singular value decomposition of the lm_head} weight matrix of a transformer-based large language model -- requiring only five lines of PyTorch and no model inference -- reveals interpretable semantic subspaces directly from the model weights. Each left singular vector identifies the vocabulary tokens most readily selected when the hidden state aligns with the corresponding singular direction; inspecting these clusters exposes the model's training data composition and curation philosophy.
  Analysing GPT-OSS-120B, Gemma-2-2B, and Qwen2.5-1.5B, we find that singular value spectra and vocabulary cluster structures differ systematically across models: GPT exhibits a graduated hierarchy of functionally differentiated subspaces; Gemma is dominated by pre-nineteenth-century English orthography, forming a stepwise clustering structure that may contribute to high output controllability; and Qwen exhibits broad multilingual coverage alongside subspaces whose vocabulary the authors have determined to be ethically inappropriate for direct publication.
  Base-instruct comparison reveals that ethically concerning subspaces originate in pretraining and are not removed by post-training alignment. We introduce the Vocabulary Cluster Score (VCS) to quantify subspace coherence, and the Weighted Projection Score (WPS) as a static glitch token detector; applying WPS to GPT-OSS-120B recovers shokubutsu-hyakka-tsu (ID 137606), a well-known glitch token widely reported in the CJK language community, without any model inference. We propose a taxonomy of root causes for problematic vocabulary content and call for lm_head} SVD analysis to be adopted as a standard pre-release safety auditing step. Our findings further suggest directions toward SVD-guided tokenizer optimisation and more controllable LLM design.

Despite substantial progress enabled by deep learning, designing TSC models that are both accurate and interpretable remains a challenging task. Many existing approaches adopt a direct feature-to-label classification paradigm, by collapsing high-dimensional temporal embeddings into class logits via a single linear projection (often after global pooling), the paradigm conflates feature extraction and decision logic into an inseparable mapping.
  To address these limitations, we propose PDFTime, a prototype-guided framework that reformulates time series classification as a multi-stage decision process. Instead of direct feature-to-label mapping, PDFTime leverages learned prototypes to approximate class-conditional feature distributions in the latent space, enabling progressive discrimination through classification sub-tasks of varying granularity. To our knowledge, PDFTime is the first framework to reformulate time series classification as a decoupled, multi-stage similarity-based reasoning process, breaking the long-standing paradigm of direct, black-box feature-to-label mapping. Extensive evaluations demonstrate that PDFTime achieves state-of-the-art (SOTA) performance across UEA and UCR benchmarks. ### [214] [From Reasoning Chains to Verifiable Subproblems: Curriculum Reinforcement Learning Enables Credit Assignment for LLM Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22074)
*Xitai Jiang,Zihan Tang,Wenze Lin,Yang Yue,Shenzhi Wang,Gao Huang*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: SCRL通过从参考推理链中提取可验证的子问题，固定原始问题为最终子问题，并采用子问题级别的归一化方法，独立对每个子问题位置进行奖励归一化，将优势值分配给对应答案片段，实现无需外部评分或奖励模型的细粒度信用分配。

Conclusion: SCRL通过构建子问题课程并引入子问题级归一化，有效解决了困难推理问题中的梯度死亡问题，显著提升了大模型在复杂推理任务中的性能，尤其在高难度问题上表现突出。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning from verifiable rewards (RLVR) has shown strong promise for LLM reasoning, but outcome-based RLVR remains inefficient on hard problems because correct final-answer rollouts are rare and sample-level credit assignment cannot use partial progress in failed attempts. We introduce SCRL (Subproblem Curriculum Reinforcement Learning), a curriculum RL framework that derives verifiable subproblems from reference reasoning chains and fixes the final subproblem as the original problem. This turns partial progress on hard problems into verifiable learning signals. Algorithmically, SCRL uses subproblem-level normalization, which normalizes rewards independently at each subproblem position and assigns the resulting advantages to the corresponding answer spans, enabling finer-grained credit assignment without external rubrics or reward models. Our analysis shows that subproblem curricula lift hard problems out of gradient dead zones, with larger relative gains as the original problem becomes harder. Across seven mathematical reasoning benchmarks, SCRL outperforms strong curriculum-learning baselines, improving average accuracy over GRPO by +4.1 points on Qwen3-4B-Base and +1.9 points on Qwen3-14B-Base. On AIME24, AIME25, and IMO-Bench, SCRL further improves pass@1 by +3.7 points and pass@64 by +4.6 points on Qwen3-4B-Base, indicating better exploration on hard reasoning problems.

The efficacy of the approach is demonstrated through the reconstruction of aerodynamic loads on the Great Belt East Bridge, simulated under a linear unsteady assumption. Abstract: Symbolic methods are generally not considered competitive with strong modern learners on realistic supervised tasks. *Shuo Yang,Jinda Lu,Kexin Huang,Chiyu Ma,Shaohang Wei,Yuyang Liu,Guoyin Wang,Jingren Zhou,Li Yuan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出OWPO方法，通过解耦优化方向与更新幅度，利用不对称重加权实现加速对齐和增益锁定，结合迭代参考更新形成“棘轮效应”，显著提升RLVR训练效率与稳定性，超越现有基线方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有RLVR方法因二元验证器奖励稀疏性导致训练效率低且不稳定；传统基于参考策略的令牌级约束会无差别惩罚偏差，可能反转验证器判断方向，抑制性能提升。

Method: 提出One-Way Policy Optimization（OWPO），将验证器决定更新方向，参考策略仅调节更新幅度；采用非对称重加权：对劣于参考的偏差进行加速对齐，对优于参考的偏差实施增益锁定；结合迭代参考更新，形成持续巩固优势的‘棘轮效应’。

Result: 实验表明，OWPO在多个任务上优于DAPO、OPD、MOPD等强基线，突破固定先验瓶颈，实现无需依赖外部参考模型的持续自我进化。

Conclusion: OWPO通过解耦优化方向与幅度，有效缓解奖励稀疏带来的训练不稳定性，实现更高效、更稳定的自进化能力，为LLM推理能力扩展提供新范式。

Abstract: Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) has become a promising paradigm for scaling reasoning capabilities of Large Language Models (LLMs). However, the sparsity of binary verifier rewards often leads to low efficiency and optimization instability. To stabilize training, existing methods typically impose token-level constraints relative to a reference policy. We identify that such constraints penalize deviations indiscriminately; this can flip verifier-determined direction when the policy attempts to outperform the reference, thereby suppressing gains. To resolve this, we propose One-Way Policy Optimization (OWPO), a method based on the principle of decoupling optimization direction from update magnitude. In OWPO, the verifier dictates the update direction, while the reference policy serves only to adjust the magnitude. Specifically, OWPO applies asymmetric reweighting: it performs Accelerated Alignment for inferior deviations (where the policy lags behind the reference) and Gain Locking for superior deviations (where the policy surpasses the reference). Furthermore, by incorporating iterative reference updates, OWPO creates a ``Ratchet Effect'' that continuously consolidates gains. Experimental results demonstrate that OWPO outperforms strong baselines, including DAPO, OPD, and MOPD, breaking the bottleneck of fixed priors to enable continuous self-evolution without reliance on external reference models.

</details>


### [218] [Beyond Euclidean Proximity: Repairing Latent World Models with Horizon-Matched Trajectory Reachability Metrics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22164)
*Liangyu Li,Shengzhi Wang,Qingwen Liu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出轨迹可达性度量（TRM），一种针对固定潜在世界模型的后处理终端排序方法，通过训练小型成对头利用日志轨迹结构替代或混合原始潜在距离作为成本函数，显著提升长时程规划成功率；在TwoRoom基准上，从7.0%提升至97.0%，且机制分析表明原始潜在距离虽包含高可解性信息但误排序，而TRM能有效捕捉关键状态信号并改善规划器选择的终点顺序。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统潜在模型中的终端成本接口因依赖原始潜在距离进行候选序列排序，可能引入错误的相关信息，导致规划器做出次优决策；尤其在长时程任务中，潜在空间的欧氏距离无法准确反映可达性，需更精准的终端评估机制。

Method: 提出轨迹可达性度量（TRM），使用从历史轨迹数据中学习的小型成对分类头，基于广义、平衡的时间间隔进行训练，实现对潜在状态序列末端的可达性评估，并可作为独立或混合成本用于规划阶段，保持原有模型结构不变。

Result: 在TwoRoom硬基准测试中，原始潜在规划成功率为7.0%，全时程TRM提升至97.0%；相同方法将PLDM基线从32.7%提升至84.0%；短时程TRM仅达35.0%；机械分析显示，尽管位置信息在潜在空间中高度可解（R²=0.998），但原始潜在距离严重误排序，而TRM捕获了关键信号。在PushT任务中，TRM风格的任务状态度量更清晰地改进了SCSA排名与最终距离表现。

Conclusion: TRM是一种面向规划器的修复机制，其有效性取决于是否能正确建模终端可达性；当原始潜在距离不能可靠反映任务相关性时，应采用或补充如TRM等显式可达性度量，以增强规划质量。

Abstract: Latent world models can contain the state needed for control, yet their terminal-cost interface can expose the planner to the wrong decision-relevant information. In common latent MPC, candidate sequences are ranked by Euclidean distance between predicted terminal and goal latent states; this assumes that raw latent distance weights reachability-relevant variables correctly. We propose trajectory reachability metrics (TRM), a post-hoc terminal-ranking method for fixed latent world models. TRM trains a small pairwise head from logged trajectory structure and uses it as a replacement or hybrid cost; the encoder, dynamics, sampler, optimizer, and evaluation manifests remain fixed. The key design choice is horizon-aware supervision: the metric is trained on broad, balanced temporal separations to match the long-horizon terminal candidate ranking problem. On a hard TwoRoom benchmark, raw latent planning with LeWorldModel (LeWM) reaches 7.0% success, while full-horizon TRM reaches 97.0%; shuffled temporal-label controls stay at 0.0%. The same recipe improves a PLDM baseline from 32.7% to 84.0% across three seeds, and a short-horizon TRM variant reaches only 35.0% with the 100,000 pair budget. In TwoRoom, we provide mechanistic evidence for why TRM works: XY position is linearly decodable (R^2=0.998), yet raw latent MSE misranks candidates; the XY-probe rowspace accounts for less than 1% of terminal-goal latent MSE but carries most candidate-quality signal; and SCSA audits show that TRM improves the ordering and selected endpoint seen by the planner. On PushT go50/go75, TRM-style task-state metrics improve SCSA ranking and selected final distance more cleanly than closed-loop success, motivating auxiliary hybrid costs in continuous manipulation. TRM is the planner-facing repair, and audits explain when terminal reachability metrics should replace or augment raw latent proximity.

### [219] [Maestro: Reinforcement Learning to Orchestrate Hierarchical Model-Skill Ensembles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22177)
*Jinyang Wu,Guocheng Zhai,Ruihan Jin,Yuhao Shen,Zhengxi Lu,Fan Zhang,Haoran Luo,Zheng Lian,Zhengqi Wen,Jianhua Tao*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: Maestro 是一个基于强化学习的编排框架，通过动态组合多专家模型和双层技能库来解决异构多模态任务。它不依赖单一大模型，而是训练轻量级策略以决定何时调用外部专家、选择哪个模型-技能对，以及何时终止。该方法在无需步骤级监督的情况下优化策略，并在多个基准测试中超越 GPT-5 和 Gemini-2.5-Pro。其策略具有良好的泛化能力，可适应未见过的模型与技能而无需重训，且保持高效低延迟。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有框架依赖单一大模型和固定逻辑，无法充分利用不同模型在不同领域的互补优势，导致性能受限。需要一种能动态协调多种专家模型与技能的机制。

Method: 将多模态任务建模为在分层模型-技能注册表上的序列决策问题，使用强化学习训练一个轻量级策略，动态选择专家模型与技能组合，并决定执行时机与终止条件。策略通过结果反馈进行优化，无需步骤级标注。

Result: 在十个代表性多模态基准上，仅使用4B参数的编排器，平均准确率达70.1%，优于GPT-5（69.3%）和Gemini-2.5-Pro（68.7%）。引入域外专家后，在四个挑战性任务上仍取得59.5%的平均准确率，优于所有闭源基线。系统具备高计算效率与低延迟特性。

Conclusion: Maestro 证明了通过强化学习实现灵活、高效、可泛化的多模型-多技能协同是可行的，显著提升了自主智能体在复杂多模态任务中的表现，同时具备良好的扩展性和实用性。

Abstract: The proliferation of large language models (LLMs) and modular skills has endowed autonomous agents with increasingly powerful capabilities. Existing frameworks typically rely on monolithic LLMs and fixed logic to interface with these skills. This gives rise to a critical bottleneck: different LLMs offer distinct advantages across diverse domains, yet current frameworks fail to exploit the complementary strengths of models and skills, thereby limiting their performance on downstream tasks. In this paper, we present Maestro (Multimodal Agent for Expert-Skill Targeted Reinforced Orchestration), a Reinforcement Learning (RL)-driven orchestration framework that reframes heterogeneous multimodal tasks as a sequential decision-making process over a hierarchical model-skill registry. Rather than consolidating all knowledge into a single model, Maestro trains a lightweight policy to dynamically compose ensembles of frozen expert models and a two-tier skill library, deciding at each step whether to invoke an external expert, which model-skill pair to select, and when to terminate. The policy is optimized via outcome-based RL, requiring no step-level supervision. We evaluate Maestro across ten representative multimodal benchmarks spanning mathematical reasoning, chart understanding, high-resolution perception, and domain-specific analysis. With only a 4B orchestrator, Maestro achieves an average accuracy of 70.1%, surpassing both GPT-5 (69.3%) and Gemini-2.5-Pro (68.7%). Crucially, the learned coordination policy generalizes to unseen models and skills without retraining: augmenting the registry with out-of-domain experts yields a 59.5% average on four challenging benchmarks, outperforming all closed-source baselines. Maestro further maintains high computational efficiency with low latency. The source code is available at https://github.com/jinyangwu/Maestro.

### [220] [Survive or Collapse: The Asymmetric Roles of Data Gating and Reward Grounding in Self-Play RL](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22217)
*Sophia Xiao Pu,Zhaotian Weng,Chengzhi Liu,Jayanth Srinivasa,Gaowen Liu,William Yang Wang,Xin Eric Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究自对弈强化学习中语言模型的稳定性问题，发现数据级门控（决定哪些任务进入训练池）比奖励信号对稳定性起决定性作用。通过控制实验表明，严格的数据门控可确保稳定，而无论奖励设计如何；反之，若无门控则任何奖励均无法维持稳定。作者提出‘有根基的命题者悖论’：具有真实答案访问权的命题者会加速崩溃，因其集中训练于干净任务，快速导向虚假自洽吸引子。进一步分析显示，连续门控参数ε存在两阶段相变：低ε时训练指标分离，验证准确率仍保持较高，直到ε更高才下降。结论：数据级门控是自对弈稳定性的关键约束，而非奖励校准。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自对弈强化学习虽在推理能力上取得进展，但普遍存在崩溃与不稳定性问题，现有研究多将其归因于奖励设计不当，但对根本原因理解不足。本文旨在揭示影响自对弈稳定性的核心机制，挑战主流观点，明确数据级门控的关键作用。

Method: 在两个受控任务上进行实验：一个基于Python输出预测的任务，一个确定性DSL双任务，以消除预训练先验、输出模糊性和执行器噪声的影响。系统性测试不同奖励策略与门控机制的组合，包括二元门控和连续严格度参数ε，观察训练动态与验证性能变化。

Result: 严格的数据门控足以保证所有奖励设置下的稳定性；而移除门控后，任何奖励都无法防止崩溃。存在‘有根基的命题者悖论’：拥有真实答案访问权的命题者反而加速系统崩溃。连续门控参数ε揭示了两阶段相变：训练指标在低ε下即出现分离，验证准确率则持续保持至更高ε值。

Conclusion: 自对弈稳定性主要受数据级门控控制，而非奖励设计。因此，提升稳定性应优先优化任务筛选机制，而非反复调整奖励函数。

Abstract: Self-play reinforcement learning trains language models on their own generated tasks, co-evolving a proposer and solver without human labels. Recent systems report strong reasoning gains, but collapse and instability are widely observed and poorly understood. The dominant response treats this as a reward-design problem. We argue instead that self-play stability is governed by two distinct levers: a data-level gate that decides which proposer-generated tasks enter the training pool, and the reward signal that updates the policy on tasks already admitted. Through controlled experiments on a Python output-prediction task and a deterministic-DSL twin task that strips pretraining priors, output ambiguity, and executor noise, we find the two levers are asymmetric. A strict gate is sufficient for stability under every reward variant we test, including a self-consistency reward with no access to ground truth; while no reward variant is sufficient once the gate is removed. This asymmetry exposes a counter-intuitive coupling we call the Grounded Proposer Paradox: a proposer with ground-truth access accelerates collapse faster than an ungrounded one when paired with a self-consistency solver, by concentrating training on clean tasks that form the fastest path to a spurious self-consistent attractor. Replacing the binary gate with a continuous strictness parameter $\varepsilon$ further reveals a two-stage phase transition: training-side metrics decouple at low $\varepsilon$, while validation accuracy holds until $\varepsilon$ is much higher. Data-level gating, not reward calibration, is the binding constraint on self-play stability.

</details>


### [221] [IKNO: Infinite-order Kernel Neural Operators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22182)
*Pengyuan Zhu,Ivor W. Tsang,Yueming Lyu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出无限阶核神经算子（IKNO），通过无限阶核积分构建神经算子，实现优雅的闭式有限近似。设计两种互补构造：IKNO-Vanilla基于克罗内克特征分解在乘积网格上应用全核重整化；IKNO-TP采用逐轴重整化组合的张量积形式。开发快速计算方案，在保持高效的同时实现全局信息聚合。在时变与非时变基准测试中，包括大规模工业数据集，IKNO在几乎所有数据集上均达到当前最优性能，并具备对大规模点云的可扩展性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有神经算子主要依赖一阶核积分近似，表达能力受限，亟需提升其建模灵活性和表达力。

Method: 提出无限阶核积分框架，设计IKNO-Vanilla与IKNO-TP两种构造方式，结合克罗内克分解与张量积结构，实现闭式近似与高效计算。

Result: 在多种时间依赖与非依赖任务中，包括大规模点云数据，IKNO显著优于现有方法，达到最先进性能，同时保持良好可扩展性。

Conclusion: IKNO通过无限阶核积分有效提升了神经算子的表达能力，结合高效计算机制，在多个基准上实现卓越性能，为科学计算中的神经算子建模提供了新范式。

Abstract: Neural operators have achieved significant success in modern scientific computing due to their flexibility and strong generalization capabilities. Existing models, however, primarily rely on first-order kernel integral approximations, which severely limit their expressivity. To address this, we propose the Infinite-order Kernel Neural Operator (IKNO), which constructs neural operators via infinite-order kernel integrals and admits an elegant closed-form finite approximation. We develop two complementary infinite-order neural operator constructions: IKNO-Vanilla, which applies the full-kernel resolvent on the product grid via Kronecker eigendecomposition, and IKNO-TP, an alternative tensor-product operator that composes per-axis resolvents. Furthermore, we develop fast computation schemes for both variants of IKNO, which achieve outstanding global information aggregation while maintaining high computational efficiency. Empirically, we evaluate our IKNO on both time-dependent and time-independent benchmarks with arbitrary input shapes, including large-scale industrial datasets. Extensive experiments demonstrate that the IKNO method consistently achieves the SOTA accuracy with significant improvements on nearly all benchmark datasets while maintaining scalability to very large point clouds.

### [222] [Boundary-targeted Membership Inference Attacks on Safety Classifiers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22373)
*Anthony Hughes,Alexander Goldberg,Prince Jha,Adam Perer,Nikolaos Aletras,Niloofar Mireshghallah*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究探讨了生成式AI中安全分类器的隐私风险，发现低置信度样本对成员推断攻击（MIA）具有显著敏感性。提出一种面向边界的靶向选择策略，可有效识别易受攻击的训练样本，实验表明该方法在5%假阳性率下能恢复19%的用户危机对话，是现有MIA方法的3.5倍。结果表明基于内容的过滤无效，而噪声注入可有效缓解风险。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 安全分类器虽必要，但其训练数据涉及自残、心理健康等敏感内容，存在隐私泄露风险。现有成员推断攻击（MIA）对低置信度样本的利用不足，亟需更有效的攻击与防御机制研究。

Method: 提出边界靶向选择策略，聚焦于模型置信度低且边界附近的样本，通过放大成员身份信号提升攻击效果；结合实验评估不同攻击策略在真实安全分类器上的表现。

Result: 所提方法在5%假阳性率下成功恢复19%的用户危机对话，显著优于现有MIA方法（提升3.5倍）；边界样本具有特定模式，内容过滤无法提供有效保护，但添加噪声可有效缓解攻击风险。

Conclusion: 低置信度样本是成员推断攻击的关键突破口，现有防御手段如内容过滤无效，应优先采用噪声注入等对抗性防御策略以增强安全分类器的隐私保护能力。

Abstract: Safety classifiers are essential safeguards within generative AI systems, filtering harmful content or identifying at-risk users when interacting with large language models. Despite their necessity, these models are trained on sensitive datasets including discussions of self-harm and mental health, raising important, yet poorly understood, privacy concerns. Membership inference attacks (MIAs) allow adversaries to infer membership of examples used to train models. In this work, we hypothesize that identifying the examples on which the classifier is least confident are informative for an adversary to infer membership. This reflects a localized failure of generalization, where the model relies on memorization to resolve ambiguity in the training set. To investigate this, we introduce a new boundary-targeted selection strategy that identifies low confidence examples that amplify the signal of an examples membership within a training set. Our experimental results show that an adversary can recover 19\% of the conversations a safety classifier flagged as indicating user distress, at a 5\% false-positive rate, on a classifier fine-tuned for detecting a user who may require emotional support. This is $3.5$ times more than attacking using state-of-the-art MIA methods alone. Finally, we characterize the boundary laying examples and show that content-based filtering is ineffective for protection, and existing noise strategies can effectively mitigate susceptibility of these examples.

*Jiachang Liu,Andrea Lodi*

TL;DR: 提出了一种通用的CPU-GPU框架，用于在GPU上批量处理分支定界（BnB）中的多个节点，通过高效的小型GPU操作和填充技术解决不规则节点数据结构问题，在大规模离散优化问题中实现1-2个数量级的速度提升，并保持最优解的零间隙。该框架还可扩展至收集整个Rashomon集，支持变量重要性分析和基于用户特定指标的模型选择。

Abstract: GPUs have significantly accelerated first-order methods for large-scale optimization, especially in continuous optimization. However, this success has not transferred cleanly to problems with discrete variables, combinatorial structure, and nonlinear objectives, such as certifying optimal solutions for cardinality-constrained generalized linear models. Major challenges include the sequential processing of heterogeneous nodes in branch and bound (BnB) and frequent data movement between the CPU and GPU. We propose a simple, generic, and modular CPU--GPU framework that processes multiple BnB nodes in batches on GPUs. The framework is built around a small set of GPU-efficient routines and uses padding together with lightweight custom kernels to handle irregular node data structures. Experiments show one to two orders of magnitude speedups and zero optimality gap on challenging instances. The framework can also be extended to collect the entire Rashomon set, enabling downstream statistical analysis such as variable-importance analysis and model selection under secondary user-specific measures (e.g., AUC in classification).

### [224] [Bandit Convex Optimization with Gradient Prediction Adaptivity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22191)
*Shuche Wang,Adarsh Barik,Vincent Y. F. Tan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了在带预测的凸优化问题中，利用梯度预测改进最坏情况下的后悔界。在单点反馈下，即使预测误差总和远小于时间T，仍存在Ω(√T)的下界，表明梯度估计方差会掩盖预测的收益。为此，作者提出了两阶段方差缩减乐观梯度下降（TP-VR-OPT）算法，在两点反馈设置下，其后悔界为O(√(d·𝔼[S_T]))，其中d为决策维度。该结果与信息论下界Ω(√𝔼[S_T])相匹配，证明算法在√d因子内最优。此外，还设计了自适应版本，无需预先知道期望预测误差或时间范围，并扩展至非平稳环境，实现了同时适应预测误差与比较路径长度的动态后悔界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究如何在部分反馈的在线学习框架中，通过引入梯度预测来改善最坏情况下的后悔率。特别关注预测误差对性能的影响，探索能否实现与预测质量相关的自适应后悔界。

Method: 提出两阶段方差缩减乐观梯度下降（TP-VR-OPT）算法，采用新型方差缩减梯度估计器，其方差依赖于预测误差而非梯度范数；结合自适应机制，使算法无需先验知识即可运行，并扩展至非平稳环境以获得动态后悔保证。

Result: 在两点反馈设置下，算法达到O(√(d·𝔼[S_T]))的后悔界，且信息论下界为Ω(√𝔼[S_T])，表明算法在√d因子内最优；自适应版本可处理未知预测误差和时间范围；动态后悔界同时适应预测误差与路径长度。

Conclusion: 在两点反馈下，通过方差缩减技术，可以实现与预测误差相关的最优自适应后悔界；单点反馈下则存在根本性障碍。所提方法不仅理论最优，且具备实际应用中的自适应能力，适用于非平稳环境。

Abstract: Bandit convex optimization (BCO) is a fundamental online learning framework with partial feedback, where the learner observes only the loss incurred at the chosen decision point in each round. In this work, we investigate whether optimistic gradient predictions can improve worst-case regret guarantees in a prediction-adaptive manner. Specifically, given gradient predictions $m_t$, we seek regret bounds that scale with the cumulative prediction error $S_T=\sum_{t=1}^T \|\nabla f_t(x_t)-m_t\|^2.$ We first establish a negative result: under the single-point feedback protocol, an unavoidable $Ω(\sqrt{T})$ regret lower bound persists even when $S_T=o(T)$, showing that the variance of gradient estimation fundamentally obscures the benefit of accurate predictions. To overcome this barrier, we propose \emph{Two-Point Variance-Reduced Optimistic Gradient Descent} (TP-VR-OPT) for the two-point feedback setting. The key idea is a novel variance-reduced gradient estimator whose variance scales with the prediction error rather than the gradient norm. This yields a regret bound of $O\big(\sqrt{d\,\mathbb{E}[S_T]}\big),$ where $d$ is the decision dimension. Complementing this result, we establish an information-theoretic lower bound that scales as $Ω(\sqrt{\mathbb{E}[S_T]})$, providing a fundamental characterization of the best achievable prediction-adaptive regret and showing that TP-VR-OPT is optimal up to a factor of $\sqrt d$. We further develop adaptive variants that eliminate the need for prior knowledge of $\mathbb{E}[S_T]$ or the horizon $T$, and extend our framework to non-stationary environments, establishing dynamic regret guarantees that adapt simultaneously to the cumulative prediction error and the comparator path length.

</details>


### [225] [Structured-Sparse Attention for Entity Tracking with Subquadratic Sequence Complexity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22476)
*Hangyue Zhao,Paul Caillon,Erwan Fagnou,Alexandre Allauzen*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一种针对实体跟踪任务的高效注意力机制，利用注意力的局部块对角结构，通过分块评估近似求解器风格的算子，实现亚二次复杂度 $O(n^{4/3}d)$，在保持精度的同时显著降低计算时间，比标准密集型Transformer快2.4倍，但当并行演化属性数超过注意力头数时性能下降。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有任务特定注意力机制虽能压缩Transformer深度，但密集计算仍昂贵；本文旨在通过发现注意力的强结构特性（局部块对角集中与轻量跨块残差）来提升效率。

Method: 提出基于块的分块评估方法，精确保留块内交互，将跨块交互通过简化系统传递，实现亚二次复杂度计算。

Result: 在控制性跟踪基准上，该方法在准确率上匹配密集算子，壁钟时间减少12-29%；在相同精确匹配准确率下，比紧凑密集Transformer快2.4倍。

Conclusion: 所提方法有效利用了注意力的内在结构，显著提升了长序列实体跟踪的效率，但存在属性数量超过注意力头数时性能下降的局限性。

Abstract: Entity tracking requires maintaining and updating latent states for entities and attributes over long sequences. Recent task-specific attention operators can compress deep Transformer stacks into a few layers by performing multi-hop state propagation within a single layer, but their dense evaluation remains expensive. We show that in this setting, learned attention is strongly structured: most mass concentrates in local block-diagonal neighborhoods with a light cross-block residue. Exploiting this, we derive a blockwise evaluation of a resolvent-style operator that keeps within-block interactions exact and routes cross-block interactions through a reduced system. The resulting evaluation is subquadratic in sequence length $O(n^{4/3}d)$ (and $O(n^{7/3})$ when $d\approx n$). On controlled tracking benchmarks, our method matches the dense operator's accuracy while reducing wall-clock time by $12-29\%$ under a standardized measurement protocol, and is up to $2.4 \times$ faster than a compact dense Transformer at comparable exact-match accuracy. We further provide ablations over block size and model capacity, and identify a limitation: performance collapses when the number of simultaneously evolving properties exceeds the number of attention heads.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 实验表明，在特定约束条件下，可实现对任务复杂度自适应的图操作结构的自动化构建，显著提升了问题求解的灵活性与效率。

By executing a graph of operations, thoughts of the LLM are structured as an arbitrary graph, forming the actual graph of thoughts. Originally, the graph of operations is defined manually, which requires in-depth knowledge about the solution of the problem to solve. Such a static graph of operations is rigid and therefore lacks adaptability. We propose Reinforced Graph of Thoughts (RGoT), an automated approach to the GoT prompting paradigm that leverages reinforcement learning (RL) to adaptively generate a graph of operations from a human-defined set.
